There is a miniature version of the Three Pools Mirroring the Moon in the lobby, and a pond of fat koi. The garden on the second floor is a surprise, with swings, pavilions, and a greenway leading to the Mid-Levels Forest Park. 5.1 is also very quiet.
Then let's talk about the food and beverage. The breakfast feels unexpectedly sincere. There are three or four choices for grilled sausages alone. The noodle stall has vermicelli, noodles, and wontons. There are jackfruits and watermelons in triangular slices, which are very fresh.
Our pre-sale coupons also have a set meal for 2-3 people. We went to eat it at noon that day. I can only say that it is too good value. I didn't finish it and packed it up haha.
The geographical location is too suitable for the elderly and children. Climbing is at the back, and the main entrance is Hushan Park and the reservoir. Just take what you need.
The only small suggestion is that the sanitary napkin floor drain in the room has a little smell. It seems that the exhaust function is not turned on. I don't know if it is not good? In addition, the seal of the shower room needs to be updated, and there is a little water seepage.
